 The Prime Minister's Office has approved the proposal of the Ministry of Labor related to 'universal Social Security'
 is yojana ke tahat 50 karod se zyada vetanbhogiyon ko sarkaar kii ore se pension, medical cover samet kuch suvidhaayen muhaiyaa karaayegi
 People working in agriculture will also be included in this scheme
 shram mantralay is yojana ko 2019 ke chunaav se pehle lagu karnaa chahta he
 Ministry of Finance and Ministry of Labor are working on this scheme of two lakh crore rupees
 is yojana main desh ke kul kamgaaron kaa 40% hissaa shaamil hoga
 On the other hand, 60% of the people can partially join this scheme
 bataaya ja rahaa he ki is skim ke tahat pension, matternity cover ke saath-saath medical, beemaari or berogari bhi cover hogi
 In a meeting, the Ministry of Labor has also given a presentation on the Universal Social Security Code, after which the Ministry of Finance has also agreed to the idea
 desh ke 50 karod nagarikon kohealth insurance kii suvidhadene ke liye taiyarmodikaireke elaan ke baad ab modi sarkaar ne 10 karod garib mazaduron tak saamaajik suraksha kii suvidha pahunchane kii taiyaari shuru kar di he
 It is proposed to spend more than one lakh crore annually
 garibi rekha se neeche ke takreeban 10 karod garib mazaduron ko saamaajik suraksha kii suvidha pahunchane ke liye nai saamaajik suraksha yojana laane kii taiyaari ho rahi he
 NDTV has a draft of the new policy which proposes to provide pension, unemployment allowance, maternity benefit to medical and group insurance to 10 crore poor laborers
 ise 'lebar code on soshal sicurity' naam ke kanoon ke zariye puure desh main lagu karne kii taiyaari he
 Under this new policy of the Ministry of Labor, Social Security Fund will be created in every state
 iske zarie pension, medical suvidha, matternity suvidha, berojgaare bhatta, sicknes benefit, disablement benefit, inveledity benefit, dependents benefit, provident fund kii suvidha or group insurance benefit jaisi 10 buniyadi saamaajik suraksha suvidhaon kii yojana har BPL mazdoor or uske parivaar tak pahunchane kaa prastaav he
 a gratuity fund will also be created in it
 is nai saamaajik suraksha yojana kaa phayda das karod garib mazaduron tak pahunchane par har saal 1 lakh 20 hazaar karod tak ke kharch kaa anumaan he
 The Labor Ministry suggested to the Finance Ministry that the scheme should be implemented gradually
 sabase pehle is yojana ke tahat garib tabake ke logon ko cover kiya janaa chahie
 In doing so, the ministry will require less money at the beginning of the plan
 iske baad is skim ko universal banane ke liye fund aavanton agle 5 se 10 saalon main badhaayaa ja saktaa he
 The Labor Ministry has said to keep this scheme comprehensive, so that health, employment, old age, unemployment and maternity, etc
 can be reached to 50 crore workers
 tippaniyan Explain that this is the second largest scheme of the government after the National Health Protection Scheme

 yah do ingine vaala ladaaku vimaan he, jo bhartiya vayusena kii pehali pasand he

 rafel hawa se hawa or hawa se jameen main maar karne main sakasham he

 china ke paas bhi isaki takkar kaa koi vimaan nahin he

 ek anumaan ke mutabik 40 saal main (4,32,000 rupee) ke nivesh par ritern kul raashi 1,01,55,160 rupee mil sakati he
 Actually, compounding interest in long term investment makes your small investment much bigger
 doosraa taricoumr kuch bhi ho, vittiya jaankaar aaj ke daur main mutual fund main nivesh kii hi salaah dete hai
 However, the risk is also there
 lekin agar thodi risk ke saath lambey samay tak esaypi ke jariye nivesh kiya jaae to duusare nivesh ke tareekon se ye behatar opshan sabit hoga
 In the long run, only mutual fund returns can fight inflation

 tippaniyan Sharif on Wednesday proposed a four-point 'peace initiative' with India, including the demilitarization of Kashmir and the 'unconditional and mutual withdrawal' of forces from Siachen, in a session of the UN General Assembly

 Reserve Bank of India (RBI) Governor d Subbarao said on Thursday that the RBI has no target on the level of the rupee, it will use every resource to stabilize the rupee
 unhone kaha ki bank kii maudrik niti hastantaran tej nahin he, kyonki vanijyik bank byaaj daron main katautee kaa laabh graahakon ko dene main hichak dikhaa rahe hai or banking license ke har aavedak ko ek license nahin mil saktaa he
 After the board meeting of the bank, Subbarao told reporters that the bank has no target on the exchange rate of the rupee, rather it will try to reduce the rupee fluctuations by using every tool
 haal hi main rupaya dollar ke mukaable 60 se adhik ke nichle str par pahunch gaya tha
 He said, "I cannot say anything more than the established policy of the bank
 ham utaar-chadhaav ko niyantrit karne ke liye apane paas uplabdh upkarnon kaa upyog karte hai
 We do not have an exchange rate or target plan, we try to control the volatility of the currency using all instruments
 " When asked about banking license applications, he said that there is no fixed number for the new bank and not every applicant can get one license
 aditya birla nuwo ke license kii daur main shaamil hone or uske adhyaksh kumarmangalam birla ke arabiai ke board main hone ke kaaran hiton ke sambhavit takaraav ko lekar puche gaye sawaal par subbarao ne kaha ki banking license ke liye aavedan kiya janaa ek nai ghatana he or birla board main pichley chah varshon se hai
 He said that the issue would be discussed with the government
 subbarao ne kaha ki arabiai agle teen se chaar maheene main aavednon kaa moolyankan karegaa or uske baad duusari samiti inkaa adhyayan karegi or in par faisla legi
 Expressing concern over non-performing assets, he said that proper capital has been invested in each bank
 kendriya vittamantri pi chidambaram kii yah dharna ki arabiai ko mahangaai par niyantran karne ke alaava aarthik vikaas or rojgaar srijan par bhi dhyaan dena chahie, ke bare main poochne par subbarao ne kaha ki arabiai vittiya sthirataa or audyogic vikaas ke bich santulan sthapit karne ke liye har sambhav upaay kar rahi he
 He said that it is the responsibility of the state government to curb such schemes

 On the question of a possible conflict of interest due to Aditya Birla Nuvo joining the licensing round and its chairman Kumaramangalam Birla being on the RBI board, Subbarao said that applying for a banking license is a new phenomenon and Birla Has been on the board for the last six years
 unhone kaha ki is mudde par sarkaar se vichaar vimarsh kiya jayega
 Subbarao said that RBI will evaluate the applications in the next three to four months and after that another committee will study them and take a decision on them
